<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ритм.html>ритм</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ritm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ритмичный.html>ритми́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ritmíčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ритми́чнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ритми́чней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rhythmic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with a rhythm, e.g. music</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>rhythmic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a sense of rhythm, e.g. an actor</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>measured <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">systematic, without long breaks, e.g. work</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***робот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́бот</a> (7303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs"><a href = vnd.unilang:бот.html>robot</a></i>, from both the Czech and the Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs"><a href = vnd.unilang:бот.html>robota</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbota</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hard work, slavery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> derived from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*orbh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to change or evolve status</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the predecessor to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃órbʰos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">orphan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́бот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róbot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́бота</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́боты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́ботов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:бот.html>robot</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mechanical or virtual, artificial agent</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ровесник.html>рове́сник</a> (10767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a> (1862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровный.html>ро́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róvno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>smoothly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:довольно.html>дово́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Doróga idjót dovólʹno <b>róvno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The road is quite smooth.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>evenly, regularly, uniformly</li>
<li>sharp, exactly, precisely
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приду́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девять.html>де́вять</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja pridú <b>róvno</b> v dévjatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll be there at nine sharp.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ровный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ровный.html>ро́вный</a> (2163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orvьnъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">ро́ўны</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róŭny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rávnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровный.html>ро́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róvnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ровне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровне́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ровне́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>even, level, flat, smooth</li>
<li>straight</li>
<li>equal, balanced</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A special short masculine singular form is found in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> ровён <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>ча́с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne rovjón čás</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">God forbid, you never know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the hour is not even</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ро́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>ровне́е, <a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровне́й</a>.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ровн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***ровня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ро́вня</a> (32076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ро́в</a>(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róv(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ро́в</a>(ный)</strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róv(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ending-stressed).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ро́вня</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровня́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róvnja</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rovnjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ро́вни</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровни́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ро́вни</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ро́вней</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровня.html>ровне́й</a></b>)

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровный.html>ро́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ров</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.       <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a>, сровнять, сровнить.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a> (3077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rogъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rog</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>ро́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рога́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рого́в</a></b>)
</p>
<dl><dd>N.B. |  <i>The irregular plural <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рога</a> is actually an old dual form.</i></dd></dl>
<ol><li>horn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуть.html>согну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бараний.html>бара́ний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sognútʹ v baránij <b>rog</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist smb. to one's will</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставлять.html>наставля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рога</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastavljátʹ roga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cuckold</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>ро́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изобилие.html>изоби́лия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">róg izobílija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horn of plenty, cornucopia</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>antler</li>
<li>bugle</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rogátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатка.html>рога́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rogátka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатка.html>рога́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатка.html>рога́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатка.html>рога́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>forked/Y-shaped stick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> catapult, slingshot</li>
<li>obstacle, hurdle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fourhorn sculpin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тый</a> (7753)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rogátyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>horned</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cuckolded</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rogátyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́того</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогатый.html>рога́тых</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">substance or instrument</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:роговой.html>рогова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rogovája</b> múzyka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>horn</b> music</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:роговой.html>рогова́я</a></b> обма́нка</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rogovája</b> obmánka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>horn</b>blende</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>horny <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">made of horn</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:роговой.html>рогова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rogovája</b> obolóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cornea</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>horny</b> shell</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́жа</a> (24201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rogoža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rogozia</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rogozъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reed, rush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rogóža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рогожа.html>рого́ж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>matting, burlap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">coarse fabric</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rodъ</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>ро́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>роды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>родо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>generation, birth, origin, stock, family, race</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддом</a> (18901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родильный.html>роди́льный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodílʹnyj dom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддо́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">roddóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддо́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддома́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддо́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддомо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роддом.html>роддо́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>maternity home, maternity hospital</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ródina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родинка.html>ро́динка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ródinka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родинка.html>ро́динки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родинка.html>ро́динки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родинка.html>ро́динок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> birthmark, mole, melanism, nevus (naevus) (dark spot on the skin)</li></ol>

***родить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a> (2729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rodìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give birth</li>
<li>to give rise to</li>
<li>to bear, to yield <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of land</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The usage of this verb in the imperfective is dated. Modern Russian allows only the use as a perfective.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новорожденный.html>новорождённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">novoroždjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родитель.html>роди́тель</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rodítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождение.html>рожде́ние</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">roždénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождество.html>рождество́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Roždestvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роженица.html>ро́же́ни́ца</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">róžéníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b/c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>Второ́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 4b (несов. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a>.):
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-род-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождаться.html>рожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be born
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́лся</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>родился́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> 1967 (<a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девятьсот.html>девятьсо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестьдесят.html>шестьдеся́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́м</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>году́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>rodílsja/rodilsjá</b> v 1967 (týsjača devjatʹsót šestʹdesját sedʹmóm) godú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He was born in 1967.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to arise, to come into being</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стро́йная</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>Зелёная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V lesú <b>rodílasʹ</b> jóločka, / V lesú oná roslá. / Zimój i létom strójnaja, / Zeljónaja bylá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the forest a Christmas tree <b>sprouted</b>, / In the forest it grew. / In winter and in the summer, slender / And green it was.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродиться.html>уроди́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">urodítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b/c".     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нта</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ния</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:рождаться.html>рожда́ться</a>.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> спрягается <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́пу</a> спряжения 4b (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:середина.html>середи́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>):
</p>

<p><b></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-род-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:родич.html>ро́дич</a> (20035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родич.html>ро́дич</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ródič</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родич.html>ро́дича</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родич.html>ро́дичи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родич.html>ро́дичей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>relation, relative, kindred, kinsfolk, kin</li></ol>
